< Review>
This is location number 4 for this very successful specialist craft beer chain after their Little Italy, North Park and Liberty Station locations paved the way. This branch has 20 craft beers on tap and a large selection of premium quality craft beers in bottles and cans from all over the USA including some of my favorites Alpine "Duet" IPA and Beachwood Brewing "Mango Invasive Species" IPA. I had a chat with Matt the manager and he clearly demonstrated to me that he knows his craft beers. I will certainly be popping in here in the next few days to top up my home supply. Parking is available out the front no problem. I came back a few days later and Blake gave me the best personalized service I've had anywhere in the world including Australia by helping me select a variety 6 pack of top craft IPA beers from all over the USA for only 14 bucks. I'm on my 2nd one right now....bloody fantastic ! These guys have superb on site prepared food to go with their exceptional beer selection so what else could you want ! Wow Blake even poured me a sample glass of Societe Brewing Co "The Apprentice" IPA...oh my God was it good !<//Review>

Review of the Complex:
I've lived at a few different complexes and this one is probably my favorite.

1.  Parking - I have a garage and can fit my car , lifted truck, tools, and a few spare parts. Additionally, there are plenty of spots on the street so parking is never really an issue. This was one of the biggest problems I've experienced at most places, but not here.

< Review>
Updated Review as of Ocotber 2019:

5 stars

My initial review wasn't based on customer service, residential environment, or any related issues. It was solely based on regional management and their disruptive management. Enough of that, let's get to the actual review.

Eaves Rancho Penasquitos is located 20 minutes from Fashion Valley, La Jolla, and the North County mall, and is literally minutes from the 15 and the 56 Freeway. The residence and environment is quiet and peaceful. They are pet friendly. After speaking to many of the residents, despite being pet friendly, they have never heard a dog bark unrelentingly or have seen dog poop in the common areas. The property is well-maintained and has the amenities that anyone would want, you can read them for yourself on their website. If you are looking for an apartment that is centrally located and I believe is competitively priced, you may want to consider giving them a call.

Currently, the local staff at the residence and the new manager are incredible. Great skills, very friendly, and always willing to solve issues that come up. Despite the fact that it is not easy to solve each and everyone's problems and concerns, they always make an attempt to provide solutions, and I think that is awesome. Hopefully the current staff that theybhs e will stay in place for a while, instead of being yanked and sent elsewhere.

In closing, I just want to give a shoutout to both Tasha and Sophia in the office, as well as John in Maintenance, and one of the ladies who don't really go unnoticed, I don't know her name, she is super quiet, she always makes it a point to keep the property clean.

--

My husband and I both have not been to the dentist in some time. My husband, has been away for quite a bit longer, due to previous bad experiences with other practices. <user>110411655962160480227</user><Name>Parker G< /Name><Time>1553650651342< /Time>< Rate>

< review>
What a find!!  I was looking for a new vegan spot to try out in the Los Angeles area and this one caught my attention because it serves Italian cuisine!

I decided to give this location a try, and stopped by for lunch.  It was in a very low-key and unassuming strip mall off of Palms Blvd, and I was the only customer inside at first.  The service was prompt and friendly.  I ordered their Fettuccine Alfredo and a drink from the counter and sat at the only seating they have inside, which is a long, wooden communal table.

Despite the unassuming exterior and the small dining area inside, it was very nicely and aesthetically decorated.  The table was beautiful, and the light fixtures above lovely.  It felt peaceful and relaxing.  Additionally, the service was very quick!  They had the food out within minutes, and were attentive to any toppings I wanted added.

As for the food itself, I found it to be absolutely splendid!  The vegan Fettuccine Alfredo that I ordered was made out of some sort of cashew sauce.  Whatever it was made out of, it tasted delicious!  I liked it even more than a lot of non-vegan pastas!  A definite win for me.  Having grown up in a vegan family, I know what is good vegan food and what isn't, and can often be very picky about it.  The vegan food here definitely won me over, however, and I can't wait to try out more of their dishes!

I had a lovely visit to Julie Goes Green.  The service is quick and friendly, the interior lovely decorated, and the food healthy, vegan, and delicious!  This place is definitely extremely underrated.  I will be back again to try some of the other dishes, and look forward to it!  If you love vegan food or even just good food in general, this place is for you.  Give it a try!<//review>

< Review>
Obligatory I'm not a vegan intro.

We arrived last evening (Wednesday) around 6pm. Their solo table was filled at the time, but the wait was only about 20 minutes. The time flew by while we checked out the menu and asked the patrons what they recommended. The owner/chef was also incredibly welcoming and friendly.

We ended up ordering the buffalo cauliflower, cheese pizza, and chicken parm and loved every single one of them.

My favorite was probably the buffalo cauliflower. The familiar vinegary and hot sauce was on point. What was most impressive was the texture -- a crispy outer shell that tears just like regular wings with a nice body to it. I think one of the toughest challenges of vegan food is the issue of texture. We will definitely be returning here.</Review>
